<h5><span style="color: #339966;">အရွင္ပုညာနႏၵ ေဟာၾကားေတာ္မူေသာ တရားေတာ္မ်ား စုစည္းမွု (MP3)</span></h5>
<h3><span style="color: #ff9900;"> </span></h3>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Ashin%20Pone%20Nyar%20Nanda/0-140%20Files/0001.mp3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၁။ နိဗၺာန္ေလလား</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Ashin%20Pone%20Nyar%20Nanda/0-140%20Files/0002.mp3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၂။ နီးရက္နဲ႔ ေဝးေနၾကရတာ</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Ashin%20Pone%20Nyar%20Nanda/0-140%20Files/0003.mp3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၃။ အလွဆံုးျပင္ၾကစို႔</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Ashin%20Pone%20Nyar%20Nanda/0-140%20Files/0004.mp3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၄။ လမ္းျခင္းတူပါလွ်က္ မေရာက္ႏုိင္ၾကေသးတာ</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Ashin%20Pone%20Nyar%20Nanda/0-140%20Files/0005.mp3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၅။ လမ္းျခင္းတူေပမယ့္ မေရာက္ႏိုင္ၾကေသးတာ</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Ashin%20Pone%20Nyar%20Nanda/0-140%20Files/0006.mp3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၆။ အခ်ိန္မွီေလး ေက်းဇူးဆပ္တာပါ</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Ashin%20Pone%20Nyar%20Nanda/0-140%20Files/0007.mp3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၇။ အေၾကာင္းစံု မွ အက်ိဳးေပးစံုတယ္</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Ashin%20Pone%20Nyar%20Nanda/0-140%20Files/0008.mp3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၈။ ေသာကေအးျငိမ္း</span></a></span></p>

<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Ashin%20Pone%20Nyar%20Nanda/3-92%20Files/2008%20Jan/ThaThon%20002.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၂၀၀၈ ဇန္န၀ါရီလ တရားေတာ္မ်ား အပိုင္း(၉)</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Ashin%20Pone%20Nyar%20Nanda/3-92%20Files/2008%20Jan/ThaThon%20003.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၂၀၀၈ ဇန္န၀ါရီလ တရားေတာ္မ်ား အပိုင္း(၁၀)</span></a></span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h5><strong><span style="color: #339966;">အႏၲိမပူစ်ာ ၌ေဟာၾကားေတာ္ မူေသာဆရာေတာ္ၾကီးမ်ား၏ တရားေတာ္မ်ား</span></strong></h5>
<p><span style="color: #00ffff;">၃။ <strong>ဆရာေတာ္ အရွင္ပုညနႏၵ</strong> – ေသရဲေအာင္ၾကိဳးစားၾကပါ။</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #00ffff;">၄။ <strong>ဆရာေတာ္ ဇနိတာလကၤာရ</strong> – အေသလြတ္ရာရွာၾကပါ။ ( ၂၇.၁၀.၂၀၀၉)</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #00ffff;">၅။ <strong>ဆရာေတာ္ အဂၢဥာဏ</strong> – အႏိၲမပူစ်ာတရားေတာ္ ( ၂၈.၁၀.၂၀၀၉ ) </span></p>
<p><span style="color: #00ffff;">၆။ <strong>ဆရာေတာ္ အရွင္ေဆကိႏၵ</strong> – ဆံုးၿဖတ္ဖို ့အခ်ိန္တန္ၿပီ။</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #00ffff;">ရ။ <strong>ဆရာေတာ္ ဦးသုမဂၤလ</strong> – ေသမင္းတမန္ ( ၃၀.၁၀.၂၀၀၉ )</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #00ffff;">၈။ <strong>ဆရာေတာ္ ( Dr ) ဦးေကာ၀ိဒ</strong> – ၿမင္တတ္ၾကားတတ္ပါေစ။ ( ၃၁.၁၀.၂၀၀၉ )</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #00ffff;">၉။ <strong>ပုညာရာမေက်ာင္းတိုက</strong>္ – ကထိန္အလွဴေတာ္ ( ၁.၁၁.၂၀၀၉ )</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #00ffff;">၁၀။ <strong>ေယာဆရာေတာ</strong>္ – အသိမွန္ကန္လူ ့ေတာင္ပံ ( ၁၆.၉.၂၀၀၉ )</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #00ffff;"> ( <strong>ဆရာေတာ္ အရွင္ပုညနႏ</strong>ၵ၏ ႏွစ္ (၅၀) ၿပည့္ေရႊရတု၀ိဇာတမဂၤလာ)</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #00ffff;">၁၁။ <strong>ဆရာေတာ္ အရွင္ပုညနႏၵ</strong>၏ ႏွစ္ (၅၀) ၿပည့္ေရႊရတု၀ိဇာတမဂၤလာ သိကၡာထပ္အလွဴပြဲ</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #00ffff;">၁၂။ <strong>ဆရာေတာ္ဇနိတာလကၤာရ</strong> – ၿပဳၿပင္မ်ားမွသက္ရွည္ရ ( ၁၆.၉.၂၀၀၉)</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #00ffff;">၁၃။ တိပိဋကဆရာေတာ္မ်ားအားပူေဇာ္ပဲြႏွင့္ ေမြးေန ့လက္ေဆာင္တရားေတာ္ အရွင္ပုညနႏၵ</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #00ffff;"> ( ၁၇.၉.၂၀၀၉)</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h5><strong><span style="color: #339966;">တရားေတာ္ အမွတ္ (၃)</span></strong></h5>
<p><span style="color: #00ffff;">၁။ မဂၤလာရွိတဲ့ ေမြးေန ့အလွဴ ( ဆစ္ဒနီ )</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #00ffff;">၂။ ေဒါသမၿဖစ္ၾကနဲ ့ တရားေတာ္ ( ဆစ္ဒနီ )</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #00ffff;">၃။ ၀န္တိုၿပစ္မွား အၿပစ္မ်ား( ဆစ္ဒနီ )</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #00ffff;">၄။ တရားမွတ္တိုင္</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #00ffff;">၅။ မာနႀကီးက ကြ်န္ၿဖစ္ရ</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #00ffff;">၆။ ကိုယ္နဲ ့မဆိုင္တဲ့အသိရွိပါေစ ( ၁၂.၈.၀၉)</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #00ffff;">၇။ စုေပါင္းအလွဴႏွင့္ အေဆာင္အဦးလွဴၿခင္းမွ အက်ိဳးတရား (၁၃.၈.၂၀၀၉)</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #00ffff;">၈။ လွပတဲ့ဘ၀နဲ ့ နိဗာန္၀င္ခ်င္ (၁၃ .၈.၂၀၀၉)</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #00ffff;">၉။ စင္ၾကယ္တဲ့ ကုသိုလ္ၿခံရံေသာ ေမြးေန ့အလွဴ ( ၁၄.၀၈-၂၀၀၉ )</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #00ffff;">၁၀။ အနာဂမ္လည္းအထင္းေသးတတ္ေသးတာပဲ (၁၄.၀၈.၂၀၀၉ )</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #00ffff;">၁၁။ ဆံုးၿဖတ္ခ်က္ခိုင္ပါေစ။ (၁၅.၀၈.၂၀၀၉ )</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #00ffff;">၁၂။ ေမြးေန ့မွာပါရမီၿပည့္ေအာင္ လွဴၾကည့္မယ္။ ( ပ + ဒု )</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #00ffff;">၁၃။ ေ၀းေနေပမယ့္ အနီးဆံုးမွာပါ ( ၁၉.၀၈.၂၀၀၉ )</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #00ffff;">၁၄။ ေလာကေၾကာင္းသိၿပီးမွ လွဴၾက ( ၂၃.၀၈.၂၀၀၉ )</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #00ffff;">၁၅။ ေနတတ္ရင္ ေက်နပ္စရာ ( ၂၃.၀၈.၂၀၀၉)</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #00ffff;">၁၆။ အေဖာ္ရွာလာတာပါ ( ၂၄.၀၈.၂၀၀၉)</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
[/su_column][/su_row]
<p>&nbsp;</p>
</div>

<div id="text-17" class="widget widget_text"><h3 class="widget-title">Feed Back</h3> <div class="textwidget"><p align="justify">ဓမၼမိတ္ေဆြ အေပါင္းတို ့ မိမိတုိ ့၏ တရားစခန္း အခက္အခဲမ်ား၊ နာၾကား အၾကံျပဳ လိုေသာ တရားဓမၼမ်ား ၊ ေမးျမန္းလိုေသာ ဓမၼေမးခြန္းမ်ား ၊ website ၾကည့္ရွုနာၾကားရာ ၌ အခက္အခဲမ်ား ျဖစ္ေပၚပါက ေအာက္ပါ Form တြင္ ျဖည့္စြက္၍ ေပးပို႔ အႀကံျပဳၾကပါရန္ ေမတၱာရပ္ခံအပ္ပါသည္။</p>

<script type="text/javascript">
		jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
			
		jQuery("#preloader-rkmpol").fadeOut(1500, function () {
			jQuery("#ecf-form-rkmpol").fadeIn(300);
			});
			
			$( '.ladda-button' ).ladda( 'bind' );

			$(function() {
				
						
				// Validation
				$("#form-rkmpol").validate(
				{					
					// Rules for form validation
					rules:
					{
					name0:{required: true},email1:{required: true,email: true},message2:{required: true,minlength: 10},
							
									
					},
										
					// Messages for form validation
					messages:
					{
					name0:{required: "This field is required"},email1:{required: "This field is required"},message2:{required: "This field is required"}					},					
					// Do not change code below
					errorPlacement: function(error, element) {
						error.insertAfter(element.parent());
						},
						
					submitHandler: function (form) {
										 ecf_onsubmit(jQuery('.form-rkmpol'));
						 
						 						 
						 },
						 
					invalidHandler: function (form) {	
					  	$.ladda( 'stopAll' );
					 	},
						 
					onkeyup: false,
					onfocusout: false,
					onclick: false
					
				});
			});	
			
			
			/* Form Submit ( Ajax ) */
			function ecf_onsubmit(form){	

				if(form.attr('action')=='#'){
					
					data = {};
					eldat = [];
					data['action'] = 'ecf_deliver_mail';
					data['formid'] = '12786';
					data['security'] = '7d9762fa58';
		
		
						
					jQuery('input, textarea', form).each(function(key){
						
						items = {};
						
						if (typeof $(this).data('type') === 'undefined') { return true; }
						

						
						items['type'] = $(this).data('type');
						items['label'] = $(this).data('label');
						items['value'] = this.value;
						items['name'] = this.name;

						eldat.push(items);
							
						}); // END  form).each(function(key){
							

													

						data['allelmnt'] = JSON.stringify(eldat);

						submitForm();
				
					return false;
					
				} // End if(form.attr('action')=='#'){
				
			} // End ecf_onsubmit 
			
			// Start submitForm		
			  function submitForm() {
				  
				jQuery.ajax({
					url: 'https://www.thitsarparamisociety.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php', 
					type: 'POST',
					dataType: 'json',
					data: data, 
					success: function(data) {
				
						if(data.Ok==true) {
									// success
							$("#form-rkmpol").get(0).reset();	
								
							if(data.msg == 'redirect') {
								window.location = "http://";
								} else {
									notifyme('Your Message Submitted Successfully', 'n', 'success', 'left middle');
									}
		
							}
							else {
								$("#form-rkmpol").get(0).reset();
								notifyme(data.msg, 'n', 'error', 'left middle');
								}
								
							$.ladda( 'stopAll' );	
									
							}
						});
						
										
					} // End submitForm
	
					
			// Notify	
			  function notifyme(msg, b, typ, pos) {
				  if (b == 'n') {
					  b = 'cf-submittedrkmpol';
				  } else {
					 b = 'atcrkmpol';
				  }
				  
				  $("#"+b).gnotify(msg,{
					  style: "nbootstrap",
					  elementPosition: pos,
					  className: typ
					  });
					  
					  msg = null;
					  typ = null;
					  
					}

		});		
		</script>
